var div="EDUC";
var dstart=new Date(2010,8,27);
var aData, nftext, p1, p2, oldcolor='none', browserType;
// Variable to control Hours of Operation 
var nHrsType=1; 
// variables to control display of meals checkboxes
var nbr=1; 
var nlu=1; 
var ndi=1; 
var nla=0;
// variable to control if there is only one, unchecked, meal so it can appear  
var nonlyone=0;
// Report subheader date
var dhdr = new Date(dstart);
browserType="";
var ie=false, ff=false, ch=false, sa=false, nn=false;
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("chrome"))  {browserType= "chrome"; ch=true;}
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("firefox")) {browserType= "firefox"; ff=true;}
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("safari"))  {browserType= "safari"; sa=true;}  
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("msie 6"))  {browserType= "ie6"; ie=true;} 
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("msie 7"))  {browserType= "ie7"; ie=true;}
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("msie 8"))  {browserType= "ie8"; ie=true;}
if (browserType.length==0 && window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match("gecko"))   {browserType= "gecko"; }
if (browserType.length==0 && document.layers) {browserType = "netscape"; nn=true;} 
// variables for report
var aDays = new Array("Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday","Sunday");
var aMeals = new Array("Breakfast","Lunch","Dinner","Late Nite");
var cMeals = "BLDX";
var cMeals2 = "BLSX";
var aSelected = new Array();
// Disclaimer text var
var discltxt='The nutrient information displayed for Sodexo recipes represent the known amount of a ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'particular nutrient in a recipe.  The recipes were analyzed using the CBORD Database and ' ;
    discltxt=discltxt+'additional information from food manufacturers.  The data are averages only, and should ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'be used as a guide.<br />&nbsp;<br />';
    discltxt=discltxt+'The nutrient values are for the edible portion of the recipe.  The nutrient information ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'displayed for each item is the result of its exact preparation as stated in the recipe.  ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'Any deviation from the recipe such as product substitutions or changes to portion yield ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'will render the information, inaccurate. (Recipes are modified on occasion to better meet ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'local preference in taste, or to accommodate a variety of preparation methods.) Although ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'we strive to make the information as accurate as possible, nutrition analysis is not an ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'exact science. Various factors including diet of an animal, and food processing methods ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'influence the amounts of nutrients in food. However, we hope this information will be useful ';
    discltxt=discltxt+'to you, and assist you in your desire to achieve good health through healthful eating.';
// ************************************************************************************************************
// Nutrition Facts Window with FDA Rounding
// ©Copyright 2008-2009 David A. Greene All Rights Reserved
// ************************************************************************************************************
function nf(idx) {
   if(!ie && !ff && !sa && !ch){alert('Your browser cannot display the Nutrition Facts window.   '); return false;}
   var nvar;
   var cstr = new String(nftext);
   var obj=new Object(aData[idx]);
   // Modify values for FDA here
   var c00=obj[00]; 
   nvar=parseInt(obj[01]);                // calories 
   var c01=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=50) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
   nvar=parseInt(obj[02]);                // fat calories
   var c02=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=50) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[03]),2);     // fat
   var c03=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
   var c04=parseInt(obj[04])+'';          // %fat DV
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[05]),2);     // satfat
   var c05=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
   var c06=parseInt(obj[06])+'';          // %satfat 
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[07]),2);     // trans fat
   var c07=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
   nvar=parseInt(obj[08]);                // cholesterol
   var c08=((nvar<2) ? '0' : ((nvar>=2 && nvar<5) ? '< 5' : ''+round(nvar/5,0)*5));
   var c09=parseInt(obj[09])+'';          // cholest%
   nvar=parseInt(obj[10]);                // sodium
   var c10=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=140) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
   var c11=parseInt(obj[11])+'';          // sodium%
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[12]),2);     // carbo
   var c12=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
   var c13=parseInt(obj[13])+'';          // carbo%
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[14]),2);     // dfib
   var c14=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
   var c15=parseInt(obj[15])+'';          // dfib%
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[16]),2);     // sugars
   var c16=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[17]),2);     // protein
   var c17=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.00) ? '1'  : ''+round(nvar,0)));
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[25])/5000*100,1);  // VitA% of dv
   var c18=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[26])/60*100,1);    // VitC% of dv
   var c19=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[27])/1000*100,1);  // calcium% of dv
   var c20=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
   nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[28])/18*100,1);    // Iron% of dv
   var c21=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
   var c22=obj[22];
   var c23=obj[23]; 
   var c24='<span class="allergens">'+obj[24]+'</span>';
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~servsize~/, c00);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~c~/,        c01);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~cf~/,       c02);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~fat~/,      c03);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~fatp~/,     c04);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~sfat~/,     c05);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~sfatp~/,    c06);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~tfat~/,     c07);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~chl~/,      c08);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~chp~/,      c09);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~sod~/,      c10);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~sodp~/,     c11);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~b~/,        c12);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~bp~/,       c13);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~df~/,       c14);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~dfp~/,      c15);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~sug~/,      c16);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~pro~/,      c17);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~a~/,        c18);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~cp~/,       c19);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~up~/,       c20);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~ip~/,       c21);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~rname~/,    c22);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~rdesc~/,    c23);
   cstr=cstr.replace(/~allergen~/, c24);  
   if(ie){
      var nTop=document.body.parentElement.scrollTop+5;
      var nLeft=12;
      var basew=225;
      var basey=410;
      var w=parseInt((window.screen.deviceXDPI/window.screen.logicalXDPI)*basew);
      var h=parseInt((window.screen.deviceYDPI/window.screen.logicalYDPI)*basey);
      if(w!=basew)w=w+4;
      if(h!=basey)h=h-2;
      p1 = window.createPopup();
      var objDocument = p1.document;
      objDocument.open();
      objDocument.write(cstr);
      objDocument.close();
      p1.show(nLeft,nTop,w,h,document.body);
   } 
   else {
      var nTop=window.screenY; 
      var nLeft=window.screenX;
      var attrib='height=410,width=220,directory=0,left='+nLeft+',top='+nTop+',location=0,'+
                    'menubar=0,resizable=0,scrollbars=0,titlebar=0,toolbar=0';
      if(p2 && !p2.closed){p2.close(); p2=null;}
      p2=window.open('','',attrib,true); 
      p2.document.write(cstr);   
   }
   return true
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
// Initialize viewable divs and checked checkboxes   
function objInit() {
   if(!ie && !ff && !sa && !ch){alert('Your browser may not properly display the elements on this page. Use IE, FireFox, Chrome or Safari.'); return true;}
   var cOn =((nHrsType==1) ? "DayHrs" : "AllHrs");
   var cOff=((nHrsType==1) ? "AllHrs" : "DayHrs");
   var curstyle1='TABLE.'+cOn.toUpperCase();
   var curstyle2='TABLE.'+cOff.toUpperCase();
   var chkbr='TD.CHKBR';
   var chklu='TD.CHKLU';
   var chkdi='TD.CHKDI';
   var chkla='TD.CHKLA';
   var sht=document.styleSheets[0];
   var orules=((ie || sa || ch) ? sht.rules : sht.cssRules);
   var rule_on=((ie) ? 'inline-block' : '');
   var rule_off='none', rule_brk, rule_lun, rule_din, rule_lat;
   for (var i=0;i<orules.length;i++) {
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle1){orules[i].style.display=rule_on;}
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle2){orules[i].style.display=rule_off;}
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==chkbr && nbr==0 && nonlyone==0){orules[i].style.display=rule_off;} 
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==chklu && nlu==0 && nonlyone==0){orules[i].style.display=rule_off;} 
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==chkdi && ndi==0 && nonlyone==0){orules[i].style.display=rule_off;}
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==chkla && nla==0 && nonlyone==0){orules[i].style.display=rule_off;}
	   if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()=='TR.BRK'){rule_brk=orules[i].style.display; orules[i].style.display=rule_off; orules[i].style.display=rule_brk;}
	   if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()=='TR.LUN'){rule_lun=orules[i].style.display; orules[i].style.display=rule_off; orules[i].style.display=rule_lun;}
	   if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()=='TR.DIN'){rule_din=orules[i].style.display; orules[i].style.display=rule_off; orules[i].style.display=rule_din;}
	   if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()=='TR.LAT'){rule_lat=orules[i].style.display; orules[i].style.display=rule_off; orules[i].style.display=rule_lat;}
      if(!ie && !ff && orules[i].style.display=='inline-block'){orules[i].style.display='';}
   }
   document.getElementById("btnView").disabled=true;
   document.getElementById("btnClear").disabled=true;
   return true
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
// Auto-close Nutrition Facts windows when focus is lost
function pcls(obj){
   if(oldcolor!='none'){obj.style.color=oldcolor;}
   if(p1 && p1.isOpen){p1.hide(); p1=null;}
   if(p2 && !p2.closed){p2.close(); p2=null;}
   window.status='';
   obj.blur();
   return true;
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
// Unused currently
function price_toggle() {
   var curstyle='TD.PRICE';
   var sht=document.styleSheets[0];
   var orules=((ie || sa || ch) ? sht.rules : sht.cssRules);
   var rule_on=((ie) ? 'inline-block' : '');
   var rule_off='none';
   for (var i=0;i<orules.length;i++) { 
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle) {
         orules[i].style.display=((orules[i].style.display.toLowerCase()==rule_off) ? rule_on : rule_off);
         break;
         }
      }
   return true;
}      
// ************************************************************************************************************
// c=character, s=string
function at(c, s) {return s.indexOf(c);}       // zero based
// ************************************************************************************************************
// X is number of decimal places to round to  
function round(nval, X) {X=(isNaN(X) ? 0 : parseInt(X)); return Math.round(nval*Math.pow(10,X))/Math.pow(10,X);}          
// ************************************************************************************************************  
function	rat(c, s) {return s.lastIndexOf(c);}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function getIcons(cstr){
  // cstr contains pairs with "evg y eww1w2ec" to split into images and insert text into iFullDesc or ViewReport
  if(cstr==""){return "";}
  var ss="";
  var cimg="";
  for (var ii=0;ii<=cstr.length/2;ii+=2){
     cimg=rtrim(cstr.substr(ii,2))+'.gif';
     ss+=((ss.length !=0) ? '&nbsp;' : '')+'<img class="icon" src="'+cimg+'" />';
  }
  return ss;
}  
// ************************************************************************************************************
function	getGrams(c, s) {return s.substr(s.lastIndexOf(c));}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function rtrim(s){
   while (s.charAt(s.length-1)==' '){s=s.substring(0,s.length-1);}
   return s;
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function showDate(dd) {
   var Today = new Date();
   if (showDate.arguments.length == 1){Today = new Date(dd);}
   var months= new Array('January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December');
   var days  = new Array("Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday","Sunday");
   var dow   = Today.getDay();
   var day   = Today.getDate();
   var month = Today.getMonth();
   var year  = Today.getFullYear();
   return months[month]+" "+day+", "+year;
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function showYear() { 
   var Today=new Date(); 
   return " "+Today.getFullYear()+" "; 
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function ws(obj) {
   window.status='Click to view nutrient facts'; 
   if(oldcolor=='none'){oldcolor=obj.style.color;}
   obj.style.color = 'red';
   return true; 
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function wschk(ntype) {window.status=((ntype==1) ? "Check to include in report" : ""); return true; } 
// ************************************************************************************************************
function showToggle(mealstr) {
   var curstyle='TR.'+mealstr.toUpperCase();
   var sht=document.styleSheets[0];
   var orules=((ie || sa || ch) ? sht.rules : sht.cssRules);
   var rule_on=((ie) ? 'inline-block' : '');
   var rule_off='none';   
   for (var i=0;i<orules.length;i++) {
      if(orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle){
         orules[i].style.display=((orules[i].style.display.toLowerCase()==rule_off) ? rule_on : rule_off); break;
      }
   }
   return true;
}
// ************************************************************************************************************  
function round(number, X) { X=(isNaN(X) ? 0 : X); return Math.round(number*Math.pow(10,X))/Math.pow(10,X);}               
// ************************************************************************************************************
function clearChks(){
   for (ii=aSelected.length-1; ii>=0; ii--) {document.getElementById(aSelected[ii]).checked=false;}  
   document.getElementById("btnView").disabled=true;
   document.getElementById("btnClear").disabled=true;
   aSelected.length=0;
   return true;
}
// ************************************************************************************************************
function rptlist(ochk) {
   var ii;
   var lchk  = (ochk.checked);
   var cid   = ochk.id;
   var cday  = aDays[parseInt(cid.substr(1,1))-1];
   var cmeal = aMeals[cMeals2.indexOf(cid.substr(2,1))];
   if(lchk) {aSelected[aSelected.length]=cid;}
   else {
      for (ii=aSelected.length-1; ii>=0; ii--) {
         if (aSelected[ii]==cid) {
            aSelected.splice(ii,1);
            break;
            }
         }
      }
   var cstr="";
   document.getElementById("btnView").disabled=(aSelected.length==0);
   document.getElementById("btnClear").disabled=(aSelected.length==0);
   return true
}

function getreport(doc) {
   var d=showDate();
   dhdr = new Date(dstart);
   var x='';
   //subheaders with color
   x=x+'<tr class="trhdr"><td class="thdata" colspan="2">Calories</td><td class="thdata">Fat<br />Cal</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thdata">Fat</td><td class="thpct">Fat<br />%</td><td class="thdata">Sat Fat</td><td class="thpct">Sat<br />Fat%</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thdata"><i>Trans</i> Fat</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thdata">Chol</td><td class="thpct">Chol<br />%</td><td class="thdata">Sodium</td><td class="thpct">Sodium<br />%</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thdata">Carbs</td><td class="thpct">Carbs<br />%</td><td class="thdata">DFib</td><td class="thpct">DFib<br />%</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thdata">Sugars</td><td class="thdata">Protein</td><td class="thpct">Vit&nbsp;A<br />%</td><td class="thpct">Vit&nbsp;C<br />%</td>';
   x=x+'<td class="thpct">Calcium<br />%</td><td class="thpct">Iron<br />%</td></tr>';
   var xhdr=x; // header saved to memvar
   // create inner html for report, called by view_results()
   x='<center><table id="ptbl" class="ptbl">';
   // 22 columns, no item name
   //       item                        calories                cal from fat             fat                     
   x=x+'<col style="width:32px;"><col style="width:27px;"><col style="width:33px;"><col style="width:33px;">';
   //         fat%                     satfat                       sf%                   tfat                      
   x=x+'<col style="width:30px;"><col style="width:30px;"><col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:30px;">';
   //         chol                      chol%                      sodium                sodium%  
   x=x+'<col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:30px;"><col style="width:40px;"><col style="width:35px;">';
   //         carbs                    carbs%                       dfib                   dfib%                 
   x=x+'<col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:30px;"><col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:30px;">';
   //        sugars                    protein                      vita%                  vitc%                  
   x=x+'<col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:35px;"><col style="width:30px;"><col style="width:31px;">';
   //      calcium%                    iron%
   x=x+'<col style="width:39px;"><col style="width:30">';
   // heading
   x=x+'<tr class="trhdr" style="height:54px;"><th style="width:155px; padding:0px;" colspan="5">&nbsp;';
   x=x+'<input class="btn" type="button" name="prntIt" id="prntIt" style="width:70px;'+
       ((!ff) ? '" ' : ' padding-bottom:2px;" ')+
       'onclick="if(top.frames.length==3){top.frames[2].print(); this.blur(); return true;} else {window.print(); this.blur(); return true;}" value="Print" />&nbsp;&nbsp;'+
       '<input class="btn" type="button" name="clseIt" id="clseIt" style="width:70px;'+
       ((!ff) ? '" ' : ' padding-bottom:2px;" ')+
       'onclick="return view_results(window.document);" value="Close" /></th>';
   x=x+'<th style="font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold;" colspan="12">Nutrition Summary';
   if(div=="CORP"){x=x+'<span style="font-size:7pt; vertical-align:middle;"><br /><img class="hdr" src="v.gif"> Vegetarian&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="g.gif"> '+
                       'Vegan&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="y.gif"> Your-Health-Your-Way</span>';}
   if(div=="EDUC" || div=="SCHL"){x=x+'<span style="font-size:7pt; vertical-align:middle;"><br /><img class="hdr" src="ev.gif"> Vegetarian&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="eg.gif"> '+
                                      'Vegan&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="ew.gif"> Well-Balanced&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="ec.gif"> Carb-Friendly</span>';}
   if(div=="HEAL" || div=="SSRV"){x=x+'<span style="font-size:7pt; vertical-align:middle;"><br /><img class="hdr" src="v.gif"> Vegetarian&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="g.gif"> '+
                                      'Vegan&nbsp;&nbsp;<img class="hdr" src="w1.gif"> Wellness</span>';}
   x=x+'</th><th style="font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; width:155px;" colspan="5">'+d+'</th></tr>';
 
   // selected item rows
   // meal subtotals, 15 items (22 with %'s), 23 if Weight Watchers can be included
   // where Math.round(KCAL/50 + FAT/12 - Math.min(DFIB,4)/5) = point(s)
   var nmCalories=0;
   var nmFat=0;
   var nmCalFat=0;
   var nmSatFat=0;
   var nmTransFat=0;
   var nmChol=0;
   var nmSodium=0;
   var nmCarbo=0;
   var nmDfib=0.0;
   var nmSugars=0;
   var nmProtein=0;   
   var nmVitA=0;
   var nmVitC=0.0;
   var nmCalcium=0;
   var nmIron=0.0;
   // day subtotals
   var ndCalories=0;
   var ndCalFat=0;
   var ndFat=0;
   var ndSatFat=0;
   var ndTransFat=0;
   var ndChol=0;
   var ndSodium=0;
   var ndCarbo=0;
   var ndDfib=0.0;
   var ndSugars=0;
   var ndProtein=0;   
   var ndVitA=0;
   var ndVitC=0.0;
   var ndCalcium=0;
   var ndIron=0.0;
   // totals
   var ntCalories=0;
   var ntCalFat=0;
   var ntFat=0;
   var ntSatFat=0;
   var ntTransFat=0;
   var ntChol=0;
   var ntSodium=0;
   var ntCarbo=0;
   var ntDfib=0.0;
   var ntSugars=0;
   var ntProtein=0;   
   var ntVitA=0;
   var ntVitC=0.0;
   var ntCalcium=0;
   var ntIron=0.0;
   var nvar; 
   // aSelected.length is > 0 at this point
   aSelected.sort();
   var cm='', cmeal='', cd='', cday='', cid='';
   var cid, obj, cIcons;
   var c00, c01, c02, c03, c04, c05, c06, c07, c08, c09, c10, c11, c12, c13, c14, c15, c16, c17, c18, c19, c20, c21, c22, c23, c24, c25, c26, c27, c28, c29, c30;

   //Begin main loop 
   for (var xx=00; xx<aSelected.length; xx++) {
      cmeal=aMeals[cMeals2.indexOf(aSelected[xx].substr(2,1))];
      cday=aDays[parseInt(aSelected[xx].substr(1,1) - 1)];
      if(cd!=cday){
         if(cd!=''){
            //    if cd<>'' show daily subtotal
            x=x+'<tr class="black"><td class="black" colspan="22"></td></tr>';             
            x=x+'<tr class="totalsrow"><td class="totals"><b>'+cd.substr(0,3)+'</b></td>';                        // first cell
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndCalories,0)+'</td><td>'+round(ndCalFat,0)+'</td>';                                 // calories
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndFat,1)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndFat)/65*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';          // fat
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSatFat,1)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndSatFat)/20*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';    // satfat
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndTransFat,1)+'g</td>';                                                              // trans fat
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndChol,0)+'mg</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndChol)/300*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';      // chol
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSodium,0)+'mg</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndSodium)/2400*100, 1),0)+'%</td>'; // sodium
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndCarbo,0)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndCarbo)/300*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';     // carbs
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndDfib,0)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndDfib)/25*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';        // dfib
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSugars,0)+'g</td>';                                                                // sugars
            x=x+'<td>'+round(ndProtein,0)+'g</td>';                                                               // protein                                                        
            nvar=round(parseFloat(ndVitA)/5000*100, 1);           // vita
            if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
            if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
            if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
            if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
            if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10,0)*10;}    
            x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                            // vita%
            nvar=round(parseFloat(ndVitC)/60*100, 1);
            if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
            if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
            if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
            if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
            if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
            x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                              // vitc%
            nvar=round(parseFloat(ndCalcium)/1000*100, 1);
            if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
            if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
            if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
            if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
            if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
            x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                         // Calcium
            nvar=round(parseFloat(ndIron)/18*100, 1);
            if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
            if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
            if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
            if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
            if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
            x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td></tr>'; 
            x=x+'<tr class="black"><td class="black" colspan="22"></td></tr>';                 
            // reset daily vars
            ndCalories=0;
            ndCalFat=0;
            ndFat=0;
            ndSatFat=0;
            ndTransFat=0;
            ndChol=0;
            ndSodium=0;
            ndCarbo=0;
            ndDfib=0.0;
            ndSugars=0;
            ndProtein=0;   
            ndVitA=0;
            ndVitC=0.0;
            ndCalcium=0;
            ndIron=0.0; 
            cd='';            
         }                  
         if(cd==''){      
            //show day header 
            //********************************************************
            x=x+'<tr style="border-bottom-color:black;"><td class="dayheader" colspan="22">'+cday+' '+showDate(dhdr)+'</td></tr>';
            //subheaders with color
            x=x+xhdr;
            dhdr.setDate(dhdr.getDate()+1);
         }
         cd=cday;
         cm='';
      }
      if(cm!=cmeal || cm==''){
         //show meal header and set cm=cmeal
         //*************************************************************
         x=x+'<tr><td class="mealheader" colspan="22"><b>'+cmeal.toUpperCase()+'</b></td></tr>';
         cm=cmeal;
      }
      cid=aSelected[xx].substr(9);
      obj=new Object(aData[cid]);  
      // Modify values for FDA here
      c00=obj[00]; 
      nvar=parseInt(obj[01]);                // calories 
      c01=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=50) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
      nvar=parseInt(obj[02]);                // fat calories
      c02=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=50) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[03]),2);     // fat
      c03=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
      c04=parseInt(obj[04])+'';          // %fat DV
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[05]),2);     // satfat
      c05=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
      c06=parseInt(obj[06])+'';          // %satfat 
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[07]),2);     // trans fat
      c07=((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<5.00) ? round(round(nvar/.5,0)*.5,1) : round(nvar,0)))+'';
      nvar=parseInt(obj[08]);                // cholesterol
      c08=((nvar<2) ? '0' : ((nvar>=2 && nvar<5) ? '< 5' : ''+round(nvar/5,0)*5));
      c09=parseInt(obj[09])+'';          // cholest%
      nvar=parseInt(obj[10]);                // sodium
      c10=((nvar<5) ? 0 : ((nvar>=5 && nvar<=140) ? round(nvar/5,0)*5 : round(nvar/10,0)*10))+'';
      c11=parseInt(obj[11])+'';          // sodium%
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[12]),2);     // carbo
      c12=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
      c13=parseInt(obj[13])+'';          // carbo%
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[14]),2);     // dfib
      c14=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
      c15=parseInt(obj[15])+'';          // dfib%
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[16]),2);     // sugars
      c16=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? '< 1' : ''+round(nvar,0)));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[17]),2);     // protein
      c17=((nvar<.50) ? '0' : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.00) ? '1'  : ''+round(nvar,0)));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[25])/5000*100,1);  // VitA% of dv
      c18=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[26])/60*100,1);    // VitC% of dv
      c19=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[27])/1000*100,1);  // calcium% of dv
      c20=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[28])/18*100,1);    // Iron% of dv
      c21=((nvar<1.0) ? '0' : ((nvar<=2) ? '2' : ((nvar<=10.0) ? ''+round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0) : ((nvar<=50) ? ''+round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0) : ''+round(nvar/10,0)*10))));
      c22=obj[22];
      c23=obj[23]; 
      c24=obj[24]; 
      c29=obj[29];
      // Weight Watchers Points - not FDA rounded
      c30=Math.round((parseInt(obj[01])/50)+(parseFloat(obj[03])/12)-(Math.min(4,parseFloat(obj[14]))/5));
      cIcons=getIcons(c29); 
     
      x=x+'<tr style="background-color:#fefed8;"><td colspan="22" style="height:20px; vertical-align:middle;">';
      x=x+'<span style="margin-left:4px; text-align:left; float:left; color:#000000;"><b style="font-size:10pt; font-weight:x-bold;">'+c22+'</b>';

      x=x+'<td>'+c05+'g</td><td>'+c06+'%</td>';           // satfat and sf%dv
      x=x+'<td>'+c07+'g'+'</td>';                         // trans fat
      x=x+'<td>'+c08+'mg</td><td>'+c09+'%</td>';          // chol and %dv
      x=x+'<td>'+c10+'mg</td><td>'+c11+'%</td>';          // sodium and %dv
      x=x+'<td>'+c12+'g</td><td>'+c13+'%</td>';           // carbs and %dv
      x=x+'<td>'+c14+'g</td><td>'+c15+'%</td>';           // dfib and %dv
      x=x+'<td>'+c16+'g</td><td>'+c17+'g</td>';           // sugars and protein
      x=x+'<td>'+c18+'%</td>';                            // VitA%
      x=x+'<td>'+c19+'%</td>';                            // VitC%
      x=x+'<td>'+c20+'%</td>';                            // Calcium%
      x=x+'<td>'+c21+'%</td></tr>';                       // Iron%
      // add values to totals and subtotals
      nmCalories=parseInt(c01);
      nmCalFat  =parseInt(c02);
      nmFat     =parseFloat(c03);
      nmSatFat  =parseFloat(c05);
      nmTransFat=parseFloat(c07);
      nvar=parseInt(obj[08]);                // cholesterol     
      nmChol=((nvar<2) ? 0 : ((nvar>=2 && nvar<5) ? nvar : round(nvar/5,0)*5));
      nmSodium  =parseFloat(c10);
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[12]),2);     // carbo
      nmCarbo   =((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? round(nvar,1) : round(nvar,0)));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[14]),2);     // dfib
      nmDfib    =((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? round(nvar,1) : round(nvar,0)));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[16]),2);     // sugars
      nmSugars  =((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? round(nvar,1) : round(nvar,0)));
      nvar=round(parseFloat(obj[17]),2);     // protein
      nmProtein =((nvar<.50) ? 0 : ((nvar>=.50 && nvar<1.0) ? round(nvar,1) : round(nvar,0)));   
      // 25 thru 28 are raw values for vita, vitc, calcium, iron
      nmVitA    =parseFloat(obj[25]);
      nmVitC    =parseFloat(obj[26]);
      nmCalcium =parseFloat(obj[27]);
      nmIron    =parseFloat(obj[28]);
      // increment day subtotals
      ndCalories+=nmCalories;
      ndCalFat+=nmCalFat;
      ndFat+=nmFat;
      ndSatFat+=nmSatFat;
      ndTransFat+=nmTransFat;   
      ndChol+=nmChol;
      ndSodium+=nmSodium;     
      ndCarbo+=nmCarbo;
      ndDfib+=nmDfib;            
      ndSugars+=nmSugars; 
      ndProtein+=nmProtein; 
      ndVitA+=nmVitA;
      ndVitC+=nmVitC;
      ndCalcium+=nmCalcium;
      ndIron+=nmIron; 
      // increment totals
      ntCalories+=nmCalories;
      ntCalFat+=nmCalFat;
      ntFat+=nmFat;
      ntSatFat+=nmSatFat;
      ntTransFat+=nmTransFat;   
      ntChol+=nmChol;
      ntSodium+=nmSodium;     
      ntCarbo+=nmCarbo;
      ntDfib+=nmDfib;            
      ntSugars+=nmSugars; 
      ntProtein+=nmProtein; 
      ntVitA+=nmVitA;
      ntVitC+=nmVitC;
      ntCalcium+=nmCalcium;
      ntIron+=nmIron; 
    // End loop
   }
   
   // Final Daily Total
   x=x+'<tr class="black"><td class="black" colspan="22"></td></tr>'; 
   x=x+'<tr class="totalsrow"><td class="totals"><b>'+cd.substr(0,3)+'</b></td>';                        // first cell
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndCalories,0)+'</td><td>'+round(ndCalFat,0)+'</td>';                                 // calories
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndFat,1)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndFat)/65*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';          // fat
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSatFat,1)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndSatFat)/20*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';    // satfat
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndTransFat,1)+'g</td>';                                                              // trans fat
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndChol,0)+'mg</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndChol)/300*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';      // chol
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSodium,0)+'mg</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndSodium)/2400*100, 1),0)+'%</td>'; // sodium
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndCarbo,0)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndCarbo)/300*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';     // carbs
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndDfib,0)+'g</td><td>'+round(round(parseFloat(ndDfib)/25*100, 1),0)+'%</td>';        // dfib
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndSugars,0)+'g</td>';                                                                // sugars
   x=x+'<td>'+round(ndProtein,0)+'g</td>';                                                               // protein                                                        
   nvar=round(parseFloat(ndVitA)/5000*100, 1);           // vita
   if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
   if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
   if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
   if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
   if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10,0)*10;}    
   x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                            // vita%
   nvar=round(parseFloat(ndVitC)/60*100, 1);
   if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
   if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
   if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
   if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
   if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
   x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                              // vitc%
   nvar=round(parseFloat(ndCalcium)/1000*100, 1);
   if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
   if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}
   if(nvar>2.0 && nvar<=10){nvar=round(round(nvar/2,1)*2,0);}
   if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
   if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
   x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td>';                         // Calcium
   nvar=round(parseFloat(ndIron)/18*100, 1);
   if(nvar<1.0){nvar=0;}
   if(nvar>0.0 && nvar<=2.0){nvar=2;}

   if(nvar>10 && nvar<=50){nvar=round(round(nvar/5,1)*5,0);}
   if(nvar>50){nvar=round(nvar/10, 0)*10;}    
   x=x+'<td>'+nvar+'%</td></tr>'; 
   x=x+'<tr class="black"><td class="black" colspan="22"></td></tr>';       
   
   //subheaders with color
   x=x+xhdr;
   
   // BEGIN REPORT TOTAL LINE with Spacer line
   //x=x+'<tr class="black"><td class="black" colspan="22"></td></tr>';       
   // Totals Line

   x=x+'<td>'+round(ntCalories,0)+'</td><td>'+round(ntCalFat,0)+'</td>';                                 // calories

// *****************************************************************************************
function view_results(doc) {
   var curstyle1='DIV.MAIN';
   var curstyle2='DIV.RPT';
   var sht=doc.styleSheets[0];
   var orules=((ie || sa || ch) ? sht.rules : sht.cssRules);
   var rule_on=((ie) ? 'inline' : '');
   var rule_off='none';
   var style1=0;
   var style2=0;   
   for (var i=0;i<orules.length;i++) {
      if (orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle1) {style1=i;}
      if (orules[i].selectorText.toUpperCase()==curstyle2) {style2=i;}
   }
   
   if (orules[style1].style.display==rule_on || orules[style1].style.display=='') {
      // kill visibility of div.main, show div.rpt
      orules[style1].style.display=rule_off;
      orules[style2].style.display=rule_on;
      doc.body.style.leftmargin=1;
      doc.body.style.topmargin=1;
      if(aSelected.length>0){
         doc.getElementById("RPT").innerHTML=getreport(doc);
      }
      else {
         doc.getElementById("RPT").innerHTML='<center>&nbsp;<p>&nbsp;<p><h3>At least one menu item must be selected.<p>Click the Back button and make selections.</h3><p>';
      }
   }
   else {
      orules[style2].style.display=rule_off;
      orules[style1].style.display=rule_on;
      doc.body.style.leftmargin=0;
      doc.body.style.topmargin=0;      
      doc.getElementById("RPT").innerHTML="<center>&nbsp;<p>&nbsp;<p>&nbsp;<p>&nbsp;<p><h3>Working...</h3></center>"
   }  
   return true;
}

var __wm = (function(){
var wbPrefix = "/web/";
var wbCurrentUrl = "http://drexelcampusdining.com/monday9-27.htm";

var firstYear = 1996;
var imgWidth = 500,imgHeight = 27;
var yearImgWidth = 25,monthImgWidth = 2;
var displayDay = "27";
var displayMonth = "Oct";
var displayYear = "2010";
var prettyMonths = ["Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"];
var $D=document,$=function(n){return document.getElementById(n)};
var trackerVal,curYear = -1,curMonth = -1;
var yearTracker,monthTracker;
function showTrackers(val) {
  if (val===trackerVal) return;
  var $ipp=$("wm-ipp");
  var $y=$("displayYearEl"),$m=$("displayMonthEl"),$d=$("displayDayEl");
  if (val) {
    $ipp.className="hi";
  } else {
    $ipp.className="";
    $y.innerHTML=displayYear;$m.innerHTML=displayMonth;$d.innerHTML=displayDay;
  }
  yearTracker.style.display=val?"inline":"none";
  monthTracker.style.display=val?"inline":"none";
  trackerVal = val;
}
function getElementX2(obj) {
  var $e=jQuery(obj);
  return (typeof $e=="undefined"||typeof $e.offset=="undefined")?
    getElementX(obj):Math.round($e.offset().left);
}
function trackMouseMove(event,element) {
  var eventX = getEventX(event);
  var elementX = getElementX2(element);
  var xOff = Math.min(Math.max(0, eventX - elementX),imgWidth);
  var monthOff = xOff % yearImgWidth;

  var year = Math.floor(xOff / yearImgWidth);
  var monthOfYear = Math.min(11,Math.floor(monthOff / monthImgWidth));
  // 1 extra border pixel at the left edge of the year:
  var month = (year * 12) + monthOfYear;
  var day = monthOff % 2==1?15:1;
  var dateString = zeroPad(year + firstYear) + zeroPad(monthOfYear+1,2) +
    zeroPad(day,2) + "000000";

  $("displayYearEl").innerHTML=year+firstYear;
  $("displayMonthEl").innerHTML=prettyMonths[monthOfYear];
  // looks too jarring when it changes..
  //$("displayDayEl").innerHTML=zeroPad(day,2);
  var url = wbPrefix + dateString + '/' +  wbCurrentUrl;
  $("wm-graph-anchor").href=url;

  if(curYear != year) {
    var yrOff = year * yearImgWidth;
    yearTracker.style.left = yrOff + "px";
    curYear = year;
  }
  if(curMonth != month) {
    var mtOff = year + (month * monthImgWidth) + 1;
    monthTracker.style.left = mtOff + "px";
    curMonth = month;
  }
}
function hideToolbar() {
  $("wm-ipp").style.display="none";
}
function bootstrap() {
  var $spk=$("wm-ipp-sparkline");
  yearTracker=$D.createElement('div');
  yearTracker.className='yt';
  with(yearTracker.style){
    display='none';width=yearImgWidth+"px";height=imgHeight+"px";
  }
  monthTracker=$D.createElement('div');
  monthTracker.className='mt';
  with(monthTracker.style){
    display='none';width=monthImgWidth+"px";height=imgHeight+"px";
  }
  $spk.appendChild(yearTracker);
  $spk.appendChild(monthTracker);

  var $ipp=$("wm-ipp");
  $ipp&&disclaimElement($ipp);
}
return{st:showTrackers,mv:trackMouseMove,h:hideToolbar,bt:bootstrap};
})();//]]>
